	<body>
		<category name="Slayer COMs">
			<category name="Description">
				<comment>By Aaron0000</comment>
				<comment>Turns a dozen skins in the game into "Slayer of Crawmerax" and "Slayer of the Seraphs" class mods. Crawmerax COMs boost Shock abilities and Capacity along with boosting six tier 4/5 skills (usually), and drop from Crawmerax. Seraph COMs boost Gun Damage, Damage-over-Time resistance, and regenerate ammo, while boosting five skills that help with slaying Raid bosses (of which they drop from all Seraph Guardians. Not including Dexiduous).</comment>
				<comment>NOTE: If using BLassic (Borderlands Classic Mode), use the fix at the bottom to adjust health regen to be appropriate.</comment>
				<category name="Gibbed Codes">
					<comment>Salvador - Blanco y Turquesa [Slayer of Crawmerax: BL2(BwAAAAAwJAARAiIQYBBQ6P//AUEAwf///////////38Dwf8/AME=) ]</comment>
					<comment>- Red Herring  [Slayer of the Seraphs: BL2(BwAAAAD4NAA/An4QIBFQ6P//AUEAwf///////////38Dwf8/AME=) ]</comment>
